3. Hotel rooms smell from each other, and the smell from the room to the corridor is very strong. Someone in the next room ate leeks, and the smell of leeks came to our room. Then someone might be smoking in the hallway, maybe in the next room, and then our whole room would smell like smoke. 4. What is particularly ironic is that the room states that smoking is not allowed, but there is an ashtray. I really don‚Äôt know whether the hotel allows smoking or not. We have no objection to hotels letting people smoke, but it deprives us non-smokers of their rights. If a hotel states in advance that it is a hotel that allows smoking, it should make it clear in advance, so that non-smokers can make their own choices.
5. There is no small refrigerator in the room. At our request, one was temporarily moved from another room.
6. The service of the hotel waiters is quite enthusiastic, this cannot be denied. The location of the hotel is also good. It is located in the city center and is convenient to go everywhere. But overall, this hotel has a lot of room for improvement. In the current situation, we do not recommend it.
